 In the political battlefield of Gujarat, swords have been drawn between Congress and BJP

 lekin aisa jamini str par bilkul nahin he

 ise dekhakar lagata he ki gujarat main sirf patidaar samudaay hi rahete hai, baaki nahin
 While the Patidar community has only 16 per cent of the vote in the state, the remaining 84 per cent of the votes are from other communities
 lekin charchaa sirf patidaar patidaar patidaar kii ho rahi he, to kya baaki samudaay ko lekar raajnneetik dalon ke paas koi formula he, yaa phir unhen bhagwaan bharose chhod diya gaya he?gujarat kaa jaateey samikarngujrat kii siyasat main kareeb 52 fisadi anya pichhadaa varg (obisi) betaj badshaah he

 isamen kshatriya kareeb 16 fisadi hai

 gujarat main 7 fisadi dalit, 11 fisadi adivasee, 9 fisadi muslim or 5 fisadi main saamaanya jati ke brahman, baniyaa or anya jatiyaan shaamil hai

 gujarat main pichley kuch samay main daliton ke saath aise hamalon ke kai maamle saamne aa chuke hai
 Dalit harassment cases are common in Gujarat, but this is not going to be an issue in the upcoming assembly elections

 bharat kaa paanchvaan wicket captain mahendra singh dhoni (44) ke rup main gira
 Dhoni hit eight fours in his 43-ball innings
 chennai test kii duusari pari main shandaar doharaa shatak lagane vaale dhoni ne kohli ke saath paanchaven wicket ke liye 56 ranon kii saajhedaari kii
 Ravindra Jadeja (10), who has done wonders with the ball, disappointed
 isi tarah ravichandran aswin (1) saste main out hue
 The comments harbhajan singh (0) khaataa tak nahin khol sake
 After Bhajji's dismissal, India lost the wicket of Kohli (34) on a total of 491 runs
 kohli ne apni 93 gendon kii sanyamit pari me teen chauke lagaae
 During this innings, Kohli completed 1000 runs in Test matches with two runs scored
 kohli ne apane kariyar ke 16wein test kii 27veen pari main yah mukaam hasil kiya he
 India's final wicket fell as Bhuvneshwar Kumar (10)
 isi ke saath chaaykaal kii ghoshnaa hui
 However, by the end of the day, Ashwin had roped in David Warner (26) and Phil Hughes (0)
 warner ne 56 gendon kii tej pari main teen chauke or ek chakka lagaaya
 Warner's wicket fell to a total of 56 and Hughes was also dismissed on this total
 salaami ballebaaj aid kowan 26 ranon par naabad laute jabaki shen watson ne nau ran banaae hai
 Watson has hit a six off 27 balls
 kowan ne apni 100 gendon kii sanyamit pari main chaar chauke jade hai
 Earlier, the Indian team scored 503 runs in their first innings
 bharat ke liye cheteshwar pujaara (204) or murali vijay (167) ne shandaar shatkeey paariyaan khelin
 In this way, India achieved a significant lead of 266 runs compared to the first innings
 australia kii ore se apana pehla test khel rahe glen maxwell ne chaar wicket liye jabaki jevier dorthi ne teen wicket hasil kiye
 James Pattinson had two successes
 ek wicket peter sidle ko bhi mila
 India had scored 311 runs for the loss of one wicket till stumps on the second day on Sunday
 tisare din bhartiya pari kii shuruyaat murali (129) or pujaara (162) ne kii
 Playing with restraint, Murali surpassed his highest total in Test matches (139) but he was caught by Max Cowell at the hands of Ed Cowan for a total of 387 runs
 murali ne apni 361 gendon kii marathon pari main 23 chauke or do chakke lagaae
 Murali and Pujara shared a record 370 runs for the second wicket
 murali ke out hone ke baad sachin tendulkar wicket par aae
 It was in Sachin's presence that Pujara completed his second double century of his career
 pujaara ne isse pehle 2010 main ahmedabad main england ke khilaaf 206 ranon kii naabad pari kheli thi
 During his innings, Pujara also completed 1000 runs in Test matches
 pujaara ne apane kariyar ke 11wein test kii 18veen pari main yah mukaam hasil kiya he
 He is the second fastest Indian to score 1000 runs in terms of innings while he is the fastest Indian to reach this point in terms of Test matches
 test maichon main sabase kam pariyon main 1000 ran banane vaale bhartiya vinod kambali hai
 Kambli achieved this position in 14 innings of 12 matches
 jahaan tak sabase kam test maichon main yah mukaam hasil karne kii baat he to pujaara se pehle yah ricard sunil gavaskar ke naam tha, jinhone 11 maichon kii 21 pariyon main 1000 ran banaae the
 Sachin and Pujara were batting very well but at a total of 393 runs, Pujara attempted to hook a high rising ball from James Pattinson and was caught by Xavier Dorthy
 pujaara ne apni 341 gendon kii pari main 30 chauke or ek chakka lagaaya
 Sachin was in rhythm but despite this, he scored seven runs and was caught by Matthew Wade on the back of the wicket off Pattinson, just after lunch on a total of 404 runs
 bharat kaa paanchvaan wicket captain mahendra singh dhoni (44) ke rup main gira
 Dhoni hit eight fours in his 43-ball innings
 chennai test kii duusari pari main shandaar doharaa shatak lagane vaale dhoni ne kohli ke saath paanchaven wicket ke liye 56 ranon kii saajhedaari kii
 Ravindra Jadeja (10), who has done wonders with the ball, disappointed
 isi tarah ravichandran aswin (1) saste main out hue
 The comments harbhajan singh (0) khaataa tak nahin khol sake
 After Bhajji's dismissal, India lost the wicket of Kohli (34) on a total of 491 runs
 kohli ne apni 93 gendon kii sanyamit pari me teen chauke lagaae
 During this innings, Kohli completed 1000 runs in Test matches with two runs scored
 kohli ne apane kariyar ke 16wein test kii 27veen pari main yah mukaam hasil kiya he
 India's final wicket fell as Bhuvneshwar Kumar (10)
 isi ke saath chaaykaal kii ghoshnaa hui
 Opener Ed Cowan returned unbeaten on 26 while Shane Watson has scored nine runs
 watson ne 27 gendon par ek chakka lagaaya he
 Cowan has hit four boundaries in his 100-ball controlled innings
 isse pehle, bhartiya team ne apni pehali pari main 503 ran banaae
 Cheteshwar Pujara (204) and Murali Vijay (167) played brilliant century innings for India
 is tarah bharat ne pehali pari kii tulana main 266 ranon kii mahatvapurn badhat hasil kii
 Glenn Maxwell, playing his first Test for Australia, took four wickets while Xavier Dorthy took three wickets
 james patinson ko do safalataa mili
 Peter Siddle also got one wicket
 bharat ne duusare din ravivaar ko stamps tak ek wicket ke nuksaan par 311 ran banaae the
 The Indian innings started on the third day by Murali (129) and Pujara (162)
 murali ne sanyam ke saath khelte hue test maichon main apane sarvocch yoga (139) ko paar kiya lekin 387 ranon ke kul yoga par vah maxwell kii gend par aid kowan ke haathon lapke gaye
 Murali hit 23 fours and two sixes in his 361-ball marathon innings
 murali or pujaara ne duusare wicket ke liye ricard 370 ranon kii saajhedaari kii
 Sachin Tendulkar came on the wicket after Murali was dismissed
 sachin kii maujuudagi main hi pujaara ne apane kariyar kaa doosraa doharaa shatak puraa kiya
 Pujara had earlier played an unbeaten innings of 206 runs against England in Ahmedabad in 2010
 apni is pari ke dauraan pujaara ne test maichon main 1000 ran bhi puure kiye
 Pujara achieved this position in the 18th innings of the 11th Test of his career
 pari kii sankhya ke lihaaj se vah 1000 ran banane vaale duusare sabase tej bhartiya hai jabaki test maichon ke lihaaj se vah is mukaam par sabase tej pahunchane vaale bhartiya khilaadi hai
 Vinod Kambli is the Indian to score 1000 runs in the lowest innings in Tests
 kambali ne 12 maichon kii 14 pariyon main yah mukaam hasil kar liya tha
 As far as achieving this position in the lowest Test matches, the record before Pujara was in the name of Sunil Gavaskar, who scored 1000 runs in 21 innings of 11 matches
 sachin or pujaara kaaphi acchhee ballebaaji kar rahe the lekin 393 ranon ke kul yoga par pujaara ne james patinson kii ek oonchi uthati gend ko hook karne kaa prayaas kiya or jevier dorthi ke haathon lapke gaye
 Pujara hit 30 fours and a six in his 341-ball innings
 sachin lay main the lekin iske baavjood vah saat ran banaakar 404 ranon ke kul yoga par bhojankaal ke thik baad patinson kii gend par wicket ke peeche mathew vade ke haathon lapke gaye
 India's fifth wicket fell as captain Mahendra Singh Dhoni (44)
 dhoni ne apni 43 gendon kii pari main aath chauke lagaae
 Dhoni, who scored a brilliant double century in the second innings of the Chennai Test, shared a 56-run partnership for the fifth wicket with Kohli
 gend ke saath kamaal dikhaa chuke rabindra jadeja (10) ne niraash kiya
 Similarly, Ravichandran Ashwin (1) was out cheaply
 tippaniyan Harbhajan Singh (0) could not even open an account
 bhajji ke out hone ke baad 491 ranon ke kul yoga par bharat ne kohli (34) kaa wicket ganvaaya
 Kohli hit three fours in his 93-ball controlled innings
 apni is pari ke dauraan do ran banane ke saath kohli ne test maichon main 1000 ran puure kiye
 Kohli achieved this position in the 27th innings of the 16th Test of his career
 bharat kaa antim wicket bhubaneshwar kumaar (10) ke rup main gira
 With this, tea time was announced
